<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, 21 January 2016</span></h2>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, 27 March 2013</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YF9FRX_cp-U/UVNKVsVwv9I/AAAAAAAADeE/YXrfqGmTnO8/s320/JT1.jpeg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7382757723560395708' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='247747420279261859' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='247747420279261859'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.daveyonefamilylawman.blogspot.com/2013/03/inspiration-for-future.html'>Inspiration for the Future!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-247747420279261859' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YF9FRX_cp-U/UVNKVsVwv9I/AAAAAAAADeE/YXrfqGmTnO8/s1600/JT1.jpeg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="179" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YF9FRX_cp-U/UVNKVsVwv9I/AAAAAAAADeE/YXrfqGmTnO8/s320/JT1.jpeg" width="320" /></a></div>
<br />
My first blog here featured a picture of Baby Peter who was 
systematically abused to death by his mother and 2 lodgers, 
even though the Social Services called to his how on at least 
50 times the poor 17 moths old toddler died from as many 
injuries to his body where was he supposed to run for help?<br />
<br />
At that time and in spite of a Court order to the contrary my 
children were willfully withheld by their alienating mother which 
was going to prove to be over 5 years of Parental Alienation 
and whilst I have tried to rekindle my relationship with my 2 
once loving sons in the past year today they feel like strangers 
to me!<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-6CLSYNtu1DA/UVNLx_MITuI/AAAAAAAADec/8OWDdDbw0HQ/s1600/Maa.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="112" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-6CLSYNtu1DA/UVNLx_MITuI/AAAAAAAADec/8OWDdDbw0HQ/s200/Maa.jpg" width="200" /></a></div>
<b><i><span style="color: purple;">&nbsp;Never the less in that time I have still sought positive and 
inspirational acts by people and have put my favorites here.&nbsp;</span></i></b><br />
&nbsp;<span style="color: red;"><b>Doreen Lawrence</b>
</span><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Doreen_Lawrence">http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Doreen_Lawrence</a>Following the murder of their son in 1993, Doreen and Neville 
Lawrence believed that the Metropolitan Police investigation 
was not being conducted in a professional manner, citing 
incompetence and racism as prime flaws.[3] In 1999, after<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-imLgKvRu8hA/UVNLRYLn-eI/AAAAAAAADeU/xDKOlLFlU-g/s1600/JT2.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;"><img border="0" height="200" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-imLgKvRu8hA/UVNLRYLn-eI/AAAAAAAADeU/xDKOlLFlU-g/s200/JT2.jpg" width="127" /></a></div>
years 
of campaigning, and with the support of many in the community, 
the media[4] and politics, a wide-ranging judicial inquiry was 
established by Jack Straw, the Home Secretary. Chaired by 
Sir William MacPherson, the inquiry was to investigate the 
circumstances of Stephen's death. The public inquiry was the 
subject of intense media interest which became international 
when it concluded that the Metropolitan Police was 
"institutionally racist"[5] and that this was one of the primary 
causes of their failure to solve the case.<br />
<br />
&nbsp;Help
Pakistani schoolgirl activist<span style="color: red;"> <b>Malala Yousafzai</b>,</span>
who was shot in the head by the Taliban, has
 launched a fund to help girls in Pakistan receive
an education.

<a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-21321070">http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-21321070&nbsp;</a><br />
<br />
<span style="color: red;">&nbsp;<b>Thusha Kamaleswaran</b></span>, 
Schoolgirl Paralysed In Stockwell Gang Shooting 'Walks Again'
<a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.co.uk/2013/03/25/thusha-kamaleswaran-schoolgirl-paralysed-stockwell-gang-shooting-walks_n_2947122.html?just_reloaded=1">http://www.huffingtonpost.co.uk/2013/03/25/thusha-kamaleswaran-schoolgirl-paralysed-stockwell-gang-shooting-walks_n_2947122.html?just_reloaded=1</a><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-H80D6tOGBvY/UVNKk0IVkHI/AAAAAAAADeM/oo4cJIqgyCE/s1600/WaterPhoto.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="240" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-H80D6tOGBvY/UVNKk0IVkHI/AAAAAAAADeM/oo4cJIqgyCE/s320/WaterPhoto.jpg" width="320" /></a></div>
<br />
<div style='clear: both;'></div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, 1 May 2012</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vJ5eHPZ4P8c/T5_tTdODSxI/AAAAAAAADP8/gziGTemRAwA/s400/article-2136422-0D47632400000578-953_468x286.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7382757723560395708' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='6147703494741196057' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='6147703494741196057'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.daveyonefamilylawman.blogspot.com/2012/05/rip-baby-pone-day-maybe.html'>RIP Baby 'P'..one day maybe?</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-6147703494741196057' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vJ5eHPZ4P8c/T5_tTdODSxI/AAAAAAAADP8/gziGTemRAwA/s1600/article-2136422-0D47632400000578-953_468x286.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left:1em; margin-right:1em"><img border="0" height="244" width="400" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-vJ5eHPZ4P8c/T5_tTdODSxI/AAAAAAAADP8/gziGTemRAwA/s400/article-2136422-0D47632400000578-953_468x286.jpg" /></a></div>
<b>Damages claim: Miss Shoesmith is battling for compensation of &#163;1million after being sacked over the case of Baby P (above) who died from abuse in 2007
</b>
My first ever blog on here featured the trgic story of 17 month old Baby Peter Connelly it seems nothing was learned when the council moved on in 2007! 


<a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2136422/Haringey-council-New-child-scandal-Baby-P-authority-10-starving-children-covered-lice-taken-care.html">http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2136422/Haringey-council-New-child-scandal-Baby-P-authority-10-starving-children-covered-lice-taken-care.html</a>

<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-KiOHqlaw-Wg/T5_tgx0ye3I/AAAAAAAADQI/oTrb1mKbRAI/s1600/article-2136422-0D4470E100000578-706_233x409.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear:left; float:left;margin-right:1em; margin-bottom:1em"><img border="0" height="200" width="114" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-KiOHqlaw-Wg/T5_tgx0ye3I/AAAAAAAADQI/oTrb1mKbRAI/s200/article-2136422-0D4470E100000578-706_233x409.jpg" /></a></div>
<b>More scandal: Haringey council's former head of children's services Sharon Shoesmith (above), who was sacked over the Baby P case, presided over another child abuse crisis involving the neglect of ten youngsters
</b>

Sharon Shoesmith should have been prosecuted in my view, not compensated. If I drove a 40 ton truck on the M1 motorway and was distracted from my duties by adjusting the radio or spilling my coffee then ploughed into a car killing a 17 month old child, the press and public would be baying for blood and I would have expected a jail sentence even though it had never been my wish nor intent for this to happen. In the same way the juggernault Ms. Shouemith was in charge of and on a salary 10 times what I earned as a truck driver meant she was neglegent in allowing 2 of her officers to attend Peters home 60+ times unchecked, (this is also the number of injuries this poor little chap had on his body when found dead)anyone with even modest parental instincts would have guessed something was wrong within one or two visits!
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Tuesday, 28 February 2012</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-OQ5ncZonFck/VhK0V-YbVOI/AAAAAAAAEjo/HV-VKgZOZnI/s1600/PAS%2Bmind.png' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7382757723560395708' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='4476833698201364832' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='4476833698201364832'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.daveyonefamilylawman.blogspot.com/2012/02/in-my-life-parental-alienation.html'>In my life : Parental Alienation!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4476833698201364832' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong>I recently saw this Lennon penned and vocalised Beatles song performed by Bet Midler in the film 'For the Boys!' and whilst the lyrics did seem to fit the bill I believe the slower more edgy version by Ozzy Osbourne will have some resonance with those of us who have endured the heartache of parental alienation!</strong><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-OQ5ncZonFck/VhK0V-YbVOI/AAAAAAAAEjo/HV-VKgZOZnI/s1600/PAS%2Bmind.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-OQ5ncZonFck/VhK0V-YbVOI/AAAAAAAAEjo/HV-VKgZOZnI/s1600/PAS%2Bmind.png" /></a></div>
<div style="text-align: justify;">
<br /></div>
</div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><em><span style="color: purple;"></span></em></strong></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><em><span style="color: purple;">In spite of 'winning' the battle in Family Court and offering a second family home close by "in the best interest of my children" a process that went on to bankrupt me, my children have been withheld by the mother for 4 years 5 months! now I face the pain and anguish along with the prospect of regret my children may feel should we ever try to rekindle our relationship in the future.</span></em></strong><br />
<strong><em><span style="color: purple;"><br /></span></em></strong>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<iframe allowfullscreen="" class="YOUTUBE-iframe-video" data-thumbnail-src="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/kRgGkSPzGek/0.jpg" frameborder="0" height="266" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/kRgGkSPzGek?feature=player_embedded" width="320"></iframe></div>
<strong><em><span style="color: purple;"><br /></span></em></strong></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><br /><em><span style="color: purple;"></span></em></strong></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><em><span style="color: purple;">Today I face my second family home being reprocessed any time soon by those state backed bandits the CSA, whilst my children languish in a home ,just 100 yards away which is mortgage free and purchased with the asset of the original family home.</span></em></strong></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><br /><em><span style="color: purple;"></span></em></strong></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><br /><em><span style="color: purple;"></span></em></strong></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><br /><em><span style="color: purple;"></span></em></strong></div>
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong><em><span style="color: purple;">I would like to dedicate the final moments of the above video to all at the CSA including the Minister who is content to preside over this corrupt department. I also wonder if Lord Justice Leveson would consider putting as much effort into a true review of Family Justice once he as finished being so concerned for phone hacking?</span></em></strong></div>
<br />
<br />
<br />
<div style="text-align: center;">
<strong>I wonder if there is any significance in publishing this item on the unusual date of 29th February?</strong></div>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>

          <div class="date-outer">
        
<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, 3 November 2011</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry uncustomized-post-template' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fLrcZHnPBLs/TteGc-TeOWI/AAAAAAAADCU/x0IkAGhX31M/s200/50556_136964449671099_5603721_n.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='7382757723560395708' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='4197897458879193589' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='4197897458879193589'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://www.daveyonefamilylawmanblogspotcom.socialgo.com/magazine/read/family-justice-review–my-version_490.html'>Family Justice Review : My Version!</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-4197897458879193589' itemprop='description articleBody'>
<iframe height="315" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/udpzigT8IfU" frameborder="0" width="420"></iframe><br /><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fLrcZHnPBLs/TteGc-TeOWI/AAAAAAAADCU/x0IkAGhX31M/s1600/50556_136964449671099_5603721_n.jpg"><img style="MARGIN: 0px 10px 10px 0px; WIDTH: 191px; FLOAT: left; HEIGHT: 200px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5681157287270300002" border="0" alt="" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-fLrcZHnPBLs/TteGc-TeOWI/AAAAAAAADCU/x0IkAGhX31M/s200/50556_136964449671099_5603721_n.jpg" /></a><br /><br /><div align="center"><strong><span style="font-size:78%;color:#990000;">Dedicated to Eddie and Matthew.</span></strong></div><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2a-gJaUNeAs/TteGnLfPjOI/AAAAAAAADCg/xRxN7fsmjZU/s1600/41699_100000494475213_6940489_n.jpg"><img style="MARGIN: 0px 0px 10px 10px; WIDTH: 94px; FLOAT: right; HEIGHT: 200px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5681157462608022754" border="0" alt="" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-2a-gJaUNeAs/TteGnLfPjOI/AAAAAAAADCg/xRxN7fsmjZU/s200/41699_100000494475213_6940489_n.jpg" /></a>This Autumn The Ministry of Justice in London will publish its findings of the Family Justice Review to which I participated as part of the Partners Group who has contributed to this enquiry for the past 18 months. I have already detected a number of shortfalls, therefore I have set out my Version of how it should read from my first hand experience at entering Family Court in March 2004. My contact with Family Court Judges, Solicitors, Barristers, CAFCASS, Social Services and Police ultimately to the CSA and above all the impact this has on my Children for when this should have been &#8216;in their best interest&#8217;. Instead what I witnessed between March and October 2004 ranged from inconsistency to outright corruption. Therefore I embarked on what has become almost 8 years of research worldwide within input right across the United States, Canada, New Zealand, Australia, Singapore, Greece and a number of European Countries. I have converted my findings into a frank and honest Blog and I regard this Blog as the defining culmination by this reluctant campaign.<br /><strong><em><span style="color:#6600cc;">I hope that any shortfall in the Ministry of Justice version on the Family Justice Review can be made up from my contribution here and both could lead to this God awful law being reformed!<br /></span></em></strong>C.S.A./CAFCASS: For me The Coalition Government could make immediate savings by disbanding both of these ineffectual organisations, neither have a place in Family Justice as I will show in the following paragraphs:-<br /><br />SOCIAL SERVICES: I believe Social Services has no place in Family Court (they are ill-equipped) and rather like CAFCASS will offer the Family Judge a snapshot and spurious testimony to which a Judge feels duty bound to apply, making CAFCASS and Social Services his scapegoat for the future, to offer irreversible orders to whom nobody beyond that Judge can scrutinise.<br /><br />Social Services should only be called upon in the case where there is a &#8216;History&#8217; of Violence or Abuse prior to a couple coming to Court NOT as a weapon of false allegations once they have arrived at Court. Social Services should be left to concentrate on Child Welfare so Horror Stories, such as Baby P, Victoria Climbie and Khyra Ishaq are reduced.<br /><br />FAMILY COURT JUDGE: Of the 6 or so Judges I came before most were reasoned balanced people who even if I regard their view as against me I saw the reasoning behind it. I did however come before one patronising and biased Judge who seemed to perpetuate premise of Single Parenting and by strange coincidence at this time I read an article that said Ambitious Judges who go against the Father have greater chance of promotion and so was the case here. This D.J. reserved my case for her sole consideration but was made up to H.H.J. during the process so failed to appear at the final hearing, instead a fellow D.J. whom I regarded as her &#8216;Lacky&#8217; sat in and just went along with the biased Judges&#8217; rhetoric.<br /><br />Closed Court precludes any balance analysis of proceedings and when Jack Straw as our one time Justice Minister attempted to &#8216;Open&#8217; the Court, he was met by derision by the very Judges who should have been called to account. Camilla Cavendish, who won an award for her Family Law column in The Times, was one of the first Journalists to be invited into Family Court in Ipswich and it was clear to me that at that time the same safeguards put in place for sensitive criminal cases could apply to Civil Laws, i.e. Child A, Family XYZ or even a serial number Journalists could refer to a case when given out to news of Parliament.<br /><br />Judges either willingly or otherwise collude with Barristers and Solicitors in perpetuating this corruption where financial gain can be achieved by their Court, rarely do they benefit either party, least of all the children involved and due to the closed nature of these Courts there is no accountability (if you appeal is it likely one Judge will contradict another).<br /><strong><em><span style="color:#993399;">Money is the fuel to injustice and closed courts hide this fact from public scrutiny!</span></em></strong><br />BARRISTERS AND SOLICITORS: The moment a couple steps into the Family Solicitors office they are perpetual conflict and whilst some Solicitors claim to offer Arbitration services (mine and my ex-partners did not), this goes against the grain of what they want to do, which insures they plunder the Legal Aid system for Mum whilst rendering Dad bankrupt with no regard to the Child&#8217;s welfare as they are supposed to subscribe to in Court. The Barristers take a similar line, I spent an entire duration debating the safety of allowing my Children to ride on their Go-Karts near the Road and the last 2 minutes for me to be told to leave the Family Home! All Smoke and Mirrors I&#8217;m afraid which because claimants should they want to perpetuate false allegations, which on one occasion for me was that I was an alcoholic (in fact I drink less alcohol in a year than some do in one weekend) spurious as in fact at the time I was employed to drive 40 tonne trucks for Salisbury&#8217;s, Tesco and M &amp; S, I doubt if these would have allowed such a person to take charge of a &#163;100,000 vehicle and Loads of a similar value.<br /><strong><em><span style="color:#993399;">The Law Society, or whatever they call themselves these days, cannot make a complaint against a firm of Solicitors for fear of being sued, they do not have the teeth to regulate as they should!<br /></span></em></strong>GRANDPARENTS: At the beginning of June this year I read a copy of The Mature Times and was dismayed to learn that the Family Justice Review did not see the merit in giving Grandparents rights of contact with their Grandchildren. I am of the view that when Parents maybe in dispute and possibly separating, who better to offer stability and continuity to children than Grandparents or other Family Members where appropriate.( Thanks Sir Bob).<br />Surely this would be better then Social services making their trademark snap-shot appraisals that all too often can result in children ending up in irreversible care. The very people who Social Services and family court should be serving , the children end up living a life full on the regrets instilled by this very system. I have an example of a case where a parents dogs often barked, it turned out they had kennels so the RSPCA were called but no problems were found none the less the Social Services got wind inspected the home and an 8 year old girl was put into irreversible care even when it was later proved there was no problems here either!<br /><iframe height="315" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/4WPaE8s2Occ" frameborder="0" width="560"></iframe><br /><br />Police: The police have no role to play in family (civil) law as they can only deal with criminal law but it does illustrate the starkest discrimination the law has to offer.<br />In my case the initial court order allowed contact with my children to take place via the schools so as to avoid conflict with the mother we would each collect and return them to school at our contact times and this worked fine for over one year.Sadly , and with the help of the biased judge contact was changed so it had to take place outside the former family home. So as per the revised court order I would show up at the prescribed time and place ready to take my sons on for the evening or weekend etc, but then the mother would start withholding the youngest which caused more problems when it later turned out she was bribing him to stay whilst my eldest was almost penalised for coming with me. When I objected to my son being with held, ( he was always pleased to see me after school) the police would be called and in spite of me waving my court order almost Chamberlain style they were unable to enforce it on the mother but were happy to arrest me for breaching the peace if I did not leave confusing the old boy so by 2007 he to was with held and to this date I have not had any of the Court appointed contact and all the police will say is take the mater back to court, what is the point? Mothers are regarded as &#8216;civil&#8217; whilst Fathers are seen as criminal!<br /><br /><strong><em><span style="color:#993399;">Childhood is such a short span of time we should protect it at all costs!</span></em></strong><br /><strong><em><span style="color:#993399;"><br /></span></em></strong>Children: Children in all walks of life have been given rights in order to protect them and this is right and proper.Except, I believe, between the ages of 11 and 16 where I feel Parental responsibility should not be overruled by a child&#8217;s right when all to often they are too young to reason the ramifications. It cannot be right that a child can sue a parent for a relatively minor dispute or indeed be allowed to make false allegations just ask the teacher too!<br />However in the sacred secret world of Family Court who&#8217;s continued rhetoric is &#8221; in the children&#8217;s best interest!&#8221; seldom allow the children to be heard and all the judge has to work with is a contrived interpretation from a court reporter (SS or CAFCASS) where mother has been the dominating force so the children end up acting on her will not what they truly want which in most cases is to see as much of both parents as possible in spite of separation!<br />I will go into this more in the paragraph headed The Process further on. I do however believe that children who reach secondary school age should be given the right to alter a court order as their live will become more flexible in their teens and they may just wish o pop in and see either parent at odd times and should not be constrained by an order designed to show them routine and stability in their younger years. Also there may be times a child wants to play football and have dad there during mum&#8217;s contact and mum may want to take them to the cinema during dads contact this should be agreed amicably and not by seeking to score points off each other or try to show one parent in a better light then the other. Mothers should no longer be seen as the resident parent and father as the absent one, they should be equal in their parental responsibilities.<br /><br />PARENTAL RESPONSIBILITY: The most important role a person can have in life is that of a Parent. We all come to it with trepidation and rely on our Parents&#8217; experience to handle the initial &#8216;shock&#8217;, but by the time a second child comes along skills are gained and we feel more relaxed, but nonetheless most parents will still have their childrens&#8217; best interests at heart.<br />One of my children had a soft nature so would cry or object to the slightest thing when young. My other Son was more robust and would walk in with blood dripping from his knee from a football injury but would say nothing. As a caring Dad I would apply the same level of care to both children just in case.<br /><br />I would link PR to equal Parenting, both Parents would appear on the Birth Certificate should be subjected in law to being responsible for their Child&#8217;s Welfare to the age of 18 or leaving home/full time education. Not only in the case of nurturing, education, feeding and home security but as a child gets older and is capable of breaking the law whilst their age all to often enables them to be immune from the law and at such times I believe the Parents (BOTH) should be liable for Fines, Reparation even imprisonment in the case of a Child committing a serious offence such as Rape or Murder.<br /><br />This I believe would focus the minds of Parents from the start (and maybe would be under age Parents) that it is down to them to make the best effort to do the right thing for their children and not to enter into such an undertaking without considering such facts that could lead to legal ramifications.<br /><br /><br /><strong><em><span style="color:#993399;">I would give credit to much of my opinions on child welfare to Shaun Bailey. He is a wise head on young shoulders and certainly inspires me, I just wish others would listen to this quietly spoken champion of the young!<br /></span></em></strong>Education:<br />As a Sub-Heading to this paragraph I would seek to align School with a remit of PR. We entrust Teachers with the care and welfare of our Children for a larger part of their childhood than we see them ourselves so in respect to the Teachers and our responsibility as Parents we should share the task of instilling morals, respect and responsibility onto young minds. Children should be controlled and disciplined when needed by Parents and equally by Teachers. I would also suggest this points to the Education fraternity.<br /><br />1.Children to be monitored throughout their Primary years including Pre-School and a Report drawn up in the Final Year of Primary School that outlines an individuals&#8217; potential, so that any shortfalls are clearly identified before they move onto Secondary Education and endeavours are made to eradicate such shortfalls before the end of Year 6.<br />2.Year 6 should be seen as a preparatory year in readiness for what the Child will have to face at Secondary School and to be aware of Peer pressure, Media pressure, the importance of what they can attain from an appropriate Education, Legal Studies, so rights and ramifications can be investigated then finally Sex Education, as by age 11 children would have some understanding today.<br />3.A true appraisal of an individuals&#8217; ability assessed, so those who excel in academia can follow that route. Those who do not, should be encouraged in aspects they do excel at, such as, Sports, Arts, Music etc and so long as they are supported in the basics of Reading and Writing, should from Year 7 be directed toward vocational training so they can learn Skills and Trades more appropriate to their ability.<br />4.National Service seems to carry some form of stigma who went through it in the Post War Years. I would however, advocate those children who seek to leave School without Qualification at the earliest leaving date, should be made aware they will only be eligible for Benefit which will only be paid by attending some form of apprenticeship or Further Education culminating in the completion within a minimum 3 Year Course, that they will then leave with a recognised Qualification or Vocational Skill, otherwise the previous 3 year benefit payment will be refundable to the Educational Authority.<br />It is important that we start now as this proposal will take at least a generation to come through in real terms and a better attitude will emerge by those given this opportunity as our Citizens of the future.<br /><strong><em><span style="color:#993399;">The last question asked on the M.O.J enquiry was &#8221; What question should we have asked?&#8221; I offered the suggestion that the number of suicides attributed to failing Family Courts and CSA worldwide should be considered!</span></em></strong><br /><br /><br /><p><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-E4D0uhT0TYc/TrJ7jmS1RQI/AAAAAAAAC9E/QWH69E3XujU/s1600/David-Cameron.jpg"><img style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0px auto 10px; WIDTH: 350px; DISPLAY: block; HEIGHT: 260px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5670730732318049538" border="0" alt="" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-E4D0uhT0TYc/TrJ7jmS1RQI/AAAAAAAAC9E/QWH69E3XujU/s400/David-Cameron.jpg" /></a><br /><strong>No good wearing a purple scarf <em>Dave</em> if you don't really mean it!</strong><br /><strong>Would you prefer this;<br /></strong><a href="http://www.justice.gov.uk/downloads/publications/policy/moj/family-justice-review-final-report.pdf">http://www.justice.gov.uk/downloads/publications/policy/moj/family-justice-review-final-report.pdf</a><br /><strong>Or this? <strong><span style="font-size:180%;color:#993399;">Davey's Law!</span></strong></strong></p><br /><p><strong>THE PROCESS: FAMILY JUSTICE REFORMED: Separating Parents should BOTH be eligible for &#163;500 in Legal Aid so as to arrive at a conciliatory process for the ultimate benefit and security of the children and should submit their claims simultaneously to an Arbitration Service such as ACAS for a jointly agreed order referring to:-<br /><br />Shared Care<br />Parental Responsibility<br />Contact (Reviewable when a Child reaches Age11)<br />Residency<br />Financial Settlement and Maintenance<br />This Contract should be binding and presented to a Senior Judge who will also confirm this is Legal and Binding and up to both parties to ensure it works otherwise it is enforceable on each Parent.<br /><br />Solicitors and Barristers would not be required at this stage as there would be no disputes and therefore would not need to be perpetuated.<br /><br />Social Services and CAFCASS need not apply, unless there is a history of Violence, Abuse or threat to the Childrens&#8217; Welfare by EITHER Parent. If the Judge has any concerns he should have access to the Familys&#8217; Medical history and thereafter order an investigation so as to prevent false allegations arising at point of separation.<br /><br />Once it is made clear that this order is binding and enforceable on BOTH Parents, should they wish to return matters to Court it will have to be at the individuals&#8217; own expense as no future Legal Aid will be available and this should focus minds by all concerned to get it right first time.<br /></strong><strong><em><span style="color:#993399;">I have sought to remove the financial incentives and conflict from the Family Court so there would be very rare need for Solicitors, Barristers and social services there!<br /></span></em>Grandparents should also have rights of access after separation, but where possible to have access to coincide with the Parents Contact, but above all to be there to show support, stability and continuity to very young children.<br /><br />Childrens&#8217; Schooling should not be disrupted and both Parents should stay in close contact with the School as often as possible.<br /><br />Parents should also keep the Children with the same Family GP and notify each other of any concerns that may occur during their respective contact times.</strong><br /><br /><br /><br /><a href="http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-13825737">http://www.bbc.co.uk/news/uk-13825737</a><br />See the full version including my latest letter from the Ministry of Justice by clicking on this blogs title,now we can see what we are up against;<br /><a href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/family/8863960/Fathers-denied-a-right-to-see-children.html">http://www.telegraph.co.uk/family/8863960/Fathers-denied-a-right-to-see-children.html</a><br /><br /></p><br /><p><br /><br /><a href="http://www.google.com/hostednews/ukpress/article/ALeqM5juQe_YeTi1I4_YIQywdQh8L-aNhA?docId=N0425151320249992588A">http://www.google.com/hostednews/ukpress/article/ALeqM5juQe_YeTi1I4_YIQywdQh8L-aNhA?docId=N0425151320249992588A</a><br /><br /><a href="http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2056869/Family-law-Fathers-grandparents-denied-right-children-divorce.html?ito=feeds-newsxml">http://www.dailymail.co.uk/news/article-2056869/Family-law-Fathers-grandparents-denied-right-children-divorce.html?ito=feeds-newsxml</a><br /><iframe height="315" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/n4MGBt9I5eI" frameborder="0" width="420"></iframe><br /><br /><a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eS-DwvJfkHg/Tm9POtQpZJI/AAAAAAAAC2w/iZcT8TPlHNc/s1600/AIbEiAIAAABECOb3haL2o4K6gwEiC3ZjYXJkX3Bob3RvKihkNmRkM2M3MTFlYzNiYzUzZTljZTYzYTllMDg5MzNjYTgxNDlhMGMyMAEh6aSlc42THh-WyhsZRn-iE99aSQ.jpg"><img style="MARGIN: 0px 10px 10px 0px; WIDTH: 32px; FLOAT: left; HEIGHT: 32px; CURSOR: hand" id="BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5651823171459441810" border="0" alt="" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eS-DwvJfkHg/Tm9POtQpZJI/AAAAAAAAC2w/iZcT8TPlHNc/s400/AIbEiAIAAABECOb3haL2o4K6gwEiC3ZjYXJkX3Bob3RvKihkNmRkM2M3MTFlYzNiYzUzZTljZTYzYTllMDg5MzNjYTgxNDlhMGMyMAEh6aSlc42THh-WyhsZRn-iE99aSQ.jpg" /></a>Guido Fawkes offers a comprehensive view of British politics, but has no involvement in the Family Justice movement! <a href="http://order-order.com/">http://order-order.com/</a> </p>

<h2>Lest we forget!</h2>
<div class='widget-content'>
<a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mzCFagp-7EM'>
<img alt='Lest we forget!' height='280' id='Image4_img' src='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_OvYccni7pU8/S2r8ReYLROI/AAAAAAAABIc/5jJzD5Buxi0/S1600-R/The+Lancaster+Canada.jpg' width='400'/>
</a>
<br/>
<span class='caption'>In the year we saw the last of the World War One &#8216;Tommy&#8217;s&#8217; complete his journey on this earth and many World War Two warriors now considering how many more memorials they will attend especially in foreign lands, we appreciate what their lives and those who did not return stand for in giving us freedom of speech and a quality of life many of us take for granted and my thoughts of my late father a peace loving man facing the horror of war from the rear gunning turret of a Lancaster Bomber. (click on picture to see him arrive in the US) My Dad, Eddie (1921-1990)</span>

<h2>Family Justice review e-petition</h2>

<img alt='Family Justice review e-petition' height='197' id='Image138_img' src='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-NBpdjkDqQco/TtDtex2mzeI/AAAAAAAADB8/7hlFFU2WQi4/s1600/hemming_1.jpg' width='314'/>

<span class='caption'>Sign against it NOW!</span>

<div class='clear'></div>
<span class='widget-item-control'>
<span class='item-control blog-admin'>
<a class='quickedit' href='//www.blogger.com/rearrange?blogID=7382757723560395708&widgetType=Image&widgetId=Image138&action=editWidget&sectionId=main' onclick='return _WidgetManager._PopupConfig(document.getElementById("Image138"));' target='configImage138' title='Edit'>

    function registerGetBlogUrls() {
      gadgets.rpc.register('getBlogUrls', function() {
        var holder = {};
        
          
          
          
            holder.postFeed = "https://www.blogger.com/feeds/7382757723560395708/posts/default";

      });

<h2>Her Majesty the Queen's Christmas Message!</h2>
<div class='widget-content'>
<a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1FYc9bNLS8U'>
<img alt='Her Majesty the Queen&#39;s Christmas Message!' height='417' id='Image186_img' src='http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-H-WTieqcpO0/UOH5mN72MlI/AAAAAAAADaY/LwlcOhRDpC8/s1600/QE2.jpg' width='600'/>
</a>
